[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `ZCompressorInputStream` reads `maxCodeSize` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m directly from [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muser-controlled input [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthird byte of Z header[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- When `[0m[33mmaxCodeSize[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m31[0m[39m`, the code attempts to allocate arrays totaling ~12GB [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m][0m[39m + byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m][0m[39m + byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The default constructor chain passes `[0m[33mmemoryLimitInKiB[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m`, which disables all [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory protection checks[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The validation in `[0m[1;35mLZWInputStream.initializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` only checks lower bounds [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize >= [0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m but has no upper bound validation[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Vulnerability Chain:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Expander → [0m[1;35mCompressorStreamFactory.getSingleton[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[33mmemoryLimitInKb[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. [0m[1;35mZCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m → calls [0m[1;35mthis[0m[1;39m([0m[39minputStream, [0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Extracts maxCodeSize from input → [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m31[0m[39m range[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, [0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m → skips memory check when [0m[33mlimit[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m-1[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Allocates int[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m][0m[39m → OOM[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Strategy[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mI will implement a **defense-in-depth approach** with validation in [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mLZWInputStream.initializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to prevent excessive memory allocations:[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Primary Fix: Add Upper Bound Validation in LZWInputStream[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/lzw/LZWInputStream.java`[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Strategy:**[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Add an absolute maximum limit constant [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `MAX_ALLOWED_CODE_SIZE = [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevent integer overflow[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Add a reasonable default maximum [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `DEFAULT_MAX_CODE_SIZE = [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for when [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno memory limit is explicitly set[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Modify `[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint maxCodeSize, int memoryLimitKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to enforce [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstricter validation:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `memoryLimitKiB == [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno explicit limit[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: enforce [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`DEFAULT_MAX_CODE_SIZE` to provide secure defaults[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `memoryLimitKiB > [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexplicit limit set[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: allow up to [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MAX_ALLOWED_CODE_SIZE` but respect the memory limit check[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Always validate that maxCodeSize doesn't cause integer overflow issues[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale:**[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- With `DEFAULT_MAX_CODE_SIZE = [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m`, maximum table size = [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m20[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m048[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m576[0m[39m elements[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Memory requirement = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m048[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m576[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m bytes = 6MB [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreasonable and safe[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Real-world Z files typically use maxCodeSize ≈ [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m384KB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m provides [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheadroom[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Users who need larger limits can explicitly set a memory limit and will get [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappropriate validation[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This protects all consumers of `LZWInputStream`, not just Z format[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Non-breaking: existing code with explicit memory limits continues to work[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Secure by default: code using default constructors gets protection[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Implementation Steps:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **In LZWInputStream class, add constants:**[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add `private static final int MAX_ALLOWED_CODE_SIZE = [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m;` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mabsolute maximum [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom format spec[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add `private static final int DEFAULT_MAX_CODE_SIZE = [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m;` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreasonable default[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor secure operation[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Modify [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint maxCodeSize, int memoryLimitKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method:**[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Before line [0m[1;36m206[0m[39m, add validation:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Check `maxCodeSize > MAX_ALLOWED_CODE_SIZE` → throw IllegalArgumentException[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - When `memoryLimitKiB == [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m`, check `maxCodeSize > DEFAULT_MAX_CODE_SIZE` → [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrow IllegalArgumentException with message explaining that explicit memory limit [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis needed for larger code sizes[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep existing validations and memory limit checks[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Update error messages to be informative about the limits and how to override [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthem[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Modify [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint maxCodeSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method:**[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add check for `maxCodeSize > MAX_ALLOWED_CODE_SIZE` to prevent integer [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Update the existing validation at line [0m[1;36m181[0m[39m to include upper bound check[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why this is the optimal approach:**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Secure by Default:** The default behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno explicit memory limit[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m now has [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreasonable protection, preventing DoS attacks[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Backward Compatible:** [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing code with explicit memory limits continues to work unchanged[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Real-world Z files with typical maxCodeSize values [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m16[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m work without [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodification[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Only malicious/corrupted files with extreme values are rejected[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Defense in Depth:** Protects all consumers of LZWInputStream [0m[1;39m([0m[39mZ format, and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many other implementations[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, not just the specific entry point[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Follows Existing Patterns:** UnshrinkingInputStream uses a similar approach [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith a hardcoded [0m[33mMAX_CODE_SIZE[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m13[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Configurable:** Advanced users can still use larger code sizes by explicitly [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msetting a memory limit, maintaining flexibility[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Clear Error Messages:** When rejected, the error message explains why and how [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto override if needed[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How it preserves existing logic:**[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The core LZW decompression algorithm is unchanged[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Memory limit checking mechanism remains intact[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Validation logic is enhanced, not replaced[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All existing functionality for legitimate files is preserved[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Test files like [0m[32m"bla.tar.Z"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith maxCodeSize~[0m[1;36m16[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to work[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How it addresses the evaluation report:**[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prevents OOM with malicious [0m[33mmaxCodeSize[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m31[0m[39m by rejecting it at validation stage[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Provides secure defaults for the common case [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno explicit memory limit[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maintains the existing memory limit mechanism for advanced users[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fixes the vulnerability at the source [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLZWInputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m rather than just patching [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mone entry point[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential side effects and mitigation:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Side Effect:** Legitimate files with maxCodeSize > [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m might be rejected when [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39musing default constructors[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation:** Such files are extremely rare in practice [0m[1;39m([0m[39manalysis shows [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtypical values are [0m[1;36m14[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m16[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation:** Clear error message explains how to process such files [0m[1;39m([0m[39mset [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexplicit memory limit[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation:** The limit of [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m6MB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is generous and accommodates real-world [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39musage[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Side Effect:** Breaking change for code that processes files with maxCodeSize [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m21[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m31[0m[39m using default constructors[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation:** Such code is likely already vulnerable to OOM and should be [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfixed[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation:** Simple fix: use constructor with explicit memory limit[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation:** The security benefit outweighs the minor compatibility impact[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Reference from codebase:**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- UnshrinkingInputStream demonstrates the pattern of using a constant MAX_CODE_SIZE[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m13[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for secure operation[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The existing memory limit mechanism in [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m shows the intended [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity design[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The test [0m[1;35mtestInvalidMaxCodeSize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m shows that validation of maxCodeSize is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpected and appropriate[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
